      <p>The following is a comparison of the features of notable <a href="/wiki/Shopping_cart_software" title="Shopping cart software">shopping cart software</a> packages available. Some such shopping cart software is extensible through <a href="/wiki/Third-party_software_component" title="Third-party software component">third-party software components</a> and applications. As such, the features listed below may not encompass all possible features for a given software package. The software listed here is but a fraction of all such packages on the market.</p> 
      <p></p>
